     }\n    })\n\n    function getCookieValue(a) {\n        let b = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\\\s*' + a + '\\\\s*=\\\\s*([^;]+)');\n        return b ? b.pop() : '';\n    }\n\n    function formatTime(varSecond) {\n        let intHour = Math.floor(varSecond / 60 / 60);\n        intHour = intHour < 10 ? '0' + intHour : intHour;\n        let intMin = Math.floor((varSecond / 60) % 60);\n        intMin = intMin < 10 ? '0' + intMin : intMin;\n        let intSecond = Math.ceil(varSecond % 60);\n        intSecond = intSecond < 10 ?
